   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">
    List of
    <i>
     My Little Pony: Friendship Is Magic
    </i>
    characters
   </h1>
   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
    <div class="noprint" id="siteSub">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div>
    <div id="contentSub">
     <span class="mw-redirectedfrom">
      (Redirected from
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/index.php?title=Nightmare_Moon&amp;redirect=no" title="Nightmare Moon">
       Nightmare Moon
      </a>
      )
     </span>
    </div>
    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
     Jump to:
     <a href="#mw-head">
      navigation
     </a>
     ,
     <a href="#p-search">
      search
     </a>
    </div>
    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:My_little_pony_friendship_is_magic_group_shot_r.png">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="256" data-file-width="388" height="198" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f1/My_little_pony_friendship_is_magic_group_shot_r.png/300px-My_little_pony_friendship_is_magic_group_shot_r.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/f/f1/My_little_pony_friendship_is_magic_group_shot_r.png 1.5x" width="300"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:My_little_pony_friendship_is_magic_group_shot_r.png" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         A 2011
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/San_Diego_Comic-Con_International" title="San Diego Comic-Con International">
          Comic-Con
         </a>
         poster depicting many characters from the first season.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic" title="My Little Pony: Friendship Is Magic">
         My Little Pony: Friendship Is Magic
        </a>
       </i>
       is an
       <a href="/wiki/Animated_series" title="Animated series">
        animated television series
       </a>
       based on the
       <a href="/wiki/My_Little_Pony" title="My Little Pony">
        My Little Pony
       </a>
       toyline, created by American toy and game manufacturer
       <a href="/wiki/Hasbro" title="Hasbro">
        Hasbro
       </a>
       . It features characters and settings developed by
       <a href="/wiki/Lauren_Faust" title="Lauren Faust">
        Lauren Faust
       </a>
       , who sought to create more in-depth characters than the stereotypical "girly" icons used in previous iterations of the franchise. The series began airing on October 10, 2010 in the United States on the Hub Network cable channel, which was re-branded as
       <a href="/wiki/Discovery_Family" title="Discovery Family">
        Discovery Family
       </a>
       in October 2014.
      </p>
      <p>
       The show follows a studious
       <a href="/wiki/Unicorn" title="Unicorn">
        unicorn
       </a>
       pony named Twilight Sparkle as her mentor Princess Celestia guides her to learn about friendship in the town of Ponyville. Twilight becomes best friends with five other ponies:
       <a href="/wiki/Pony" title="Pony">
        earth ponies
       </a>
       Applejack and Pinkie Pie,
       <a href="/wiki/Pegasus" title="Pegasus">
        pegasus
       </a>
       ponies Rainbow Dash and Fluttershy, and unicorn Rarity. Each represents a different facet of friendship, and Twilight discovers herself to be a key part of the magical artifacts, the Elements of Harmony. The six ponies—collectively known as the "Mane Six"—share adventures and help out other residents of Ponyville, while working out the troublesome moments in their own friendships, eventually leading to Twilight's ascension as a
       <a href="/wiki/Winged_unicorn" title="Winged unicorn">
        winged unicorn
       </a>
       known as an alicorn.
      </p>
      <p>
       Several episodes focus on the exploits of Spike, Twilight's baby
       <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">
        dragon
       </a>
       assistant, and a younger trio of pony characters (Apple Bloom, Scootaloo, and Sweetie Belle) who call themselves the "Cutie Mark Crusaders" and share their own adventures trying to discover their talents in life and receive their "cutie marks"—a central theme of the show—until the season five episode "Crusaders of the Lost Mark". Beginning in season six, the reformed villain Starlight Glimmer also becomes a focus character.
      </p>
      <p>
       The characters have been well received by critics, and are cited as one of the reasons the series' older fans, called "
       <a href="/wiki/My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_fandom" title="My Little Pony: Friendship Is Magic fandom">
        bronies
       </a>
       ", became attracted to the show. Several background characters have been popularized by fans as well, and are further incorporated as in-jokes within the show. The series later spawned numerous spin-off media, including a
       <a href="/wiki/My_Little_Pony_(IDW_Publishing)" title="My Little Pony (IDW Publishing)">
        comic book
       </a>
       and children's book series expanding some of the characters' roles, and a spin-off film series titled
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/My_Little_Pony:_Equestria_Girls" title="My Little Pony: Equestria Girls">
         My Little Pony: Equestria Girls
        </a>
       </i>
       , where several of the television series' characters are re-envisioned as humans in a
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/High_school" title="High school">
        high school
       </a>
       setting.
      </p>

      </div>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Creation_and_conception">
        Creation and conception
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Creation and conception">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       Faust was initially hired by Hasbro to create a
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bible_(writing)" title="Bible (writing)">
        pitch bible
       </a>
       for the show, allowing her to get additional help with conceptualization.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-eqd_faust_interview_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-eqd_faust_interview-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Faust said she was "extremely skeptical" about taking the job at first because she had always found shows based on girls' toys to be boring and unrelatable.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ms_faust_2-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-ms_faust-2">
         [2]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <i>
        My Little Pony
       </i>
       was one of her favorite childhood toys,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-awn_3-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-awn-3">
         [3]
        </a>
       </sup>
       but she was disappointed that her imagination at the time was nothing like the animated shows, in which the characters, according to Faust, had "endless tea parties, giggled over nothing and defeated villains by either sharing with them or crying". With the chance to work on
       <i>
        My Little Pony
       </i>
       , she hoped to prove that "cartoons for girls don't have to be a puddle of smooshy, cutesy-wootsy, goody-two-shoeness."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ms_faust_2-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-ms_faust-2">
         [2]
        </a>
       </sup>
       To do this, she incorporated into the design of the characters and the show many elements that contradicted idealized stereotypes of girls, such as diverse personalities, the message that friends can be different and can get into arguments but still be friends, and the idea that girls should not be limited by what others say they can or can not do.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ms_faust_2-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-ms_faust-2">
         [2]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Elements of the characters' personalities and the show's settings were based on her own childhood imagination of the ponies' adventures, in part inspired by the animated shows that her brothers would watch while growing up, such as
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/The_Transformers_(TV_series)" title="The Transformers (TV series)">
         Transformers
        </a>
       </i>
       and
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/G.I._Joe:_A_Real_American_Hero_(1985_TV_series)" title="G.I. Joe: A Real American Hero (1985 TV series)">
         G.I. Joe
        </a>
       </i>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4">
        <a href="#cite_note-4">
         [4]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Faust still aimed for the characters to be "relatable" characters, using stereotypical "icons of girliness" (such as the waif or the bookworm), as to broaden the appeal of the characters for the young female audience.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-slate_5-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-slate-5">
         [5]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Main_characters">
        Main characters
        <span id="Mane_Six">
        </span>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Main characters">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       <i>
        My Little Pony: Friendship Is Magic
       </i>
       focuses on six core characters, also identified as the "Mane Six",
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6">
        <a href="#cite_note-6">
         [6]
        </a>
       </sup>
       a group of friends who are brought together by the Elements of Harmony, a set of six mystical jewels and an "unstoppable force of good"
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">
        <a href="#cite_note-7">
         [7]
        </a>
       </sup>
       that are used to defend Equestria against powerful threats. Each character was designed to represent a different element and positive aspect of friendship—honesty (Applejack), kindness (Fluttershy), laughter (Pinkie Pie), generosity (Rarity), and loyalty (Rainbow Dash)—which come together to form the sixth element of "magic" (Twilight Sparkle).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-Elements_8-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-Elements-8">
         [8]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Twilight_Sparkle">
        Twilight Sparkle
        <span id="Owlowiscious">
        </span>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Twilight Sparkle">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Tara_Strong" title="Tara Strong">
         Tara Strong
        </a>
        , singing voice by
        <a href="/wiki/Rebecca_Shoichet" title="Rebecca Shoichet">
         Rebecca Shoichet
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Twilight Sparkle is the central character of the series, based on the first generation or "G1" unicorn toy Twilight.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9">
        <a href="#cite_note-9">
         [9]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She is depicted in the show's first three seasons as a purple unicorn with a pink-streaked indigo mane, and as a
       <a href="/wiki/Winged_unicorn" title="Winged unicorn">
        winged unicorn
       </a>
       called an "alicorn" in later seasons. She takes charge of the Mane Six during their adventures and helps resolve her friends' differences. She is an intelligent, dutiful, and accomplished scholar with an avid love of learning and a studied prowess in unicorn magic such as
       <a href="/wiki/Levitation" title="Levitation">
        levitation
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Teleportation" title="Teleportation">
        teleportation
       </a>
       , and the creation of
       <a href="/wiki/Force_field_(fiction)" title="Force field (fiction)">
        force fields
       </a>
       . Director Jayson Thiessen describes her as "kind of a neurotic perfectionist" who has "a touch
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Obsessive-compulsive_disorder" title="Obsessive-compulsive disorder">
        OCD
       </a>
       ,"
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE-TS_10-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE-TS-10">
         [10]
        </a>
       </sup>
       prone to suffering from nervous breakdowns when confronted with a problem that goes against her understanding.
      </p>
      <p>
       Twilight begins the story as the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prot%C3%A9g%C3%A9e" title="Protégée">
        protégée
       </a>
       of Princess Celestia, who tasks her with studying the magical properties of friendship in Ponyville and reporting her findings. Twilight resents her assignment in the opening episodes, owing her reclusiveness to her obsession with books, but she comes to form strong friendships with the rest of the Mane Six, which she realizes is key to harnessing the Elements of Harmony. She resides with her assistant Spike and pet owl Owlowiscious (pronounced the same way as
       <a href="/wiki/Aloysius" title="Aloysius">
        Aloysius
       </a>
       <span class="nowrap">
        <span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt">
         <a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">
          /
          <span style="border-bottom:1px dotted">
           <span title="/æ/: 'a' in 'bad'">
            æ
           </span>
           <span title="'l' in 'lie'">
            l
           </span>
           <span title="/ə/: 'a' in 'about'">
            ə
           </span>
           <span title="'w' in 'wind'">
            w
           </span>
           <span title="/ɪ/: 'i' in 'kit'">
            ɪ
           </span>
           <span title="/ʃ/: 'sh' in 'shy'">
            ʃ
           </span>
           <span title="/ə/: 'a' in 'about'">
            ə
           </span>
           <span title="'s' in 'sigh'">
            s
           </span>
          </span>
          /
         </a>
        </span>
       </span>
       ) in Ponyville's Golden Oak Library, where she also serves as town librarian.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-TS_11-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-TS-11">
         [11]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Her apprenticeship to Celestia ends in the season three finale "
       <a href="/wiki/Magical_Mystery_Cure" title="Magical Mystery Cure">
        Magical Mystery Cure
       </a>
       " when, by creating new magic based on her studies of friendship, Twilight transforms into an alicorn and is crowned a princess of Equestria. Assuming the title of "Princess of Friendship", Twilight becomes responsible for spreading her teachings to propagate friendships across Equestria from the Castle of Friendship,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE52_12-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE52-12">
         [12]
        </a>
       </sup>
       a mystical castle that replaces the library after its destruction in the season four finale "
       <a href="/wiki/Twilight%27s_Kingdom" title="Twilight's Kingdom">
        Twilight's Kingdom
       </a>
       ".
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Rainbow_Dash">
        Rainbow Dash
        <span id="Tank">
        </span>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Rainbow Dash">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Ashleigh_Ball" title="Ashleigh Ball">
         Ashleigh Ball
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Rainbow Dash is a sky blue
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE-RD_13-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE-RD-13">
         [13]
        </a>
       </sup>
       pegasus with a rainbow-colored mane and tail who is based on Faust's "G1" Firefly toy,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">
        <a href="#cite_note-14">
         [14]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and shares her name with the "G3" earth pony. She is an "act first and ask questions later" pegasus obsessed with speed and adventure.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE-RD_13-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE-RD-13">
         [13]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Her goal at the series' beginning is to join her heroes, the elite Wonderbolts aerobatic team,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">
        <a href="#cite_note-15">
         [15]
        </a>
       </sup>
       which is accomplished in the season six episode "Newbie Dash" after she impresses them with her multiple heroic feats across the first five seasons. Apart from helping other pegasi manage the weather around Ponyville, she spends her time practicing flight maneuvers such as the "Sonic Rainboom", a rainbow-hued
       <a href="/wiki/Sonic_boom" title="Sonic boom">
        sonic boom
       </a>
       ; it is shown in the episode "
       <a href="/wiki/The_Cutie_Mark_Chronicles" title="The Cutie Mark Chronicles">
        The Cutie Mark Chronicles
       </a>
       " that Rainbow Dash's first Sonic Rainboom as a filly produced not only her own cutie mark, but also the rest of the Mane Six's marks. She lives with a propeller-fitted pet
       <a href="/wiki/Tortoise" title="Tortoise">
        tortoise
       </a>
       named Tank in a floating
       <a href="/wiki/Condominium" title="Condominium">
        condominium
       </a>
       of clouds called the Cloudominium,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">
        <a href="#cite_note-16">
         [16]
        </a>
       </sup>
       which is sparingly seen in the show because she "doesn't sit still for very long," according to director Jim Miller.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE-RD_13-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE-RD-13">
         [13]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Faust struggled to find a suitable aspect for Rainbow Dash's Element of Harmony, seeing the character as "self-absorbed and rather irresponsible." She eventually settled on "loyalty" because it "brought out [Rainbow Dash's] positive traits."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-Elements_8-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-Elements-8">
         [8]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Pinkie_Pie">
        Pinkie Pie
        <span id="Gummy">
        </span>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Pinkie Pie">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Libman" title="Andrea Libman">
         Andrea Libman
        </a>
        , singing voice by
        <a href="/wiki/Shannon_Chan-Kent" title="Shannon Chan-Kent">
         Shannon Chan-Kent
        </a>
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17">
         <a href="#cite_note-17">
          [note 1]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Pinkie Pie (fully named Pinkamena Diane Pie) is a pink earth pony based on the "G3" toy of the same name. Her character, summarized by Thiessen as "a frenetic sugar rush",
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">
        <a href="#cite_note-18">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       was inspired by the "G1" pegasus toy Surprise.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19">
        <a href="#cite_note-19">
         [18]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She is a live-in
       <a href="/wiki/Party_service" title="Party service">
        party planner
       </a>
       at Sugarcube Corner, a
       <a href="/wiki/Bakery" title="Bakery">
        bakery
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Confectionery_store" title="Confectionery store">
        confectionery store
       </a>
       in Ponyville that resembles a
       <a href="/wiki/Gingerbread_house" title="Gingerbread house">
        gingerbread house
       </a>
       ,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">
        <a href="#cite_note-20">
         [19]
        </a>
       </sup>
       where she also keeps a toothless baby
       <a href="/wiki/Alligator" title="Alligator">
        alligator
       </a>
       named Gummy. A comedic character raised on a "dreary rock farm", Pinkie is cheerful, energetic, and talkative. She is defined by her desire to entertain her friends by throwing parties at random times and acting as outlandish as possible;
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-PP_21-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-PP-21">
         [20]
        </a>
       </sup>
       however, she demonstrates a lack of confidence and a fear of being rejected by others,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE182_22-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE182-22">
         [21]
        </a>
       </sup>
       which is occasionally expressed by her balloon-like mane deflating. Pinkie is a source of much of the series' humor,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-PP_21-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-PP-21">
         [20]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and several of the show's "wacky gags" are kept exclusive to her.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE182_22-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE182-22">
         [21]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-faustint_23-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-faustint-23">
         [22]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Her
       <a href="/wiki/Running_gag" title="Running gag">
        running gags
       </a>
       include breaking the
       <a href="/wiki/Fourth_wall" title="Fourth wall">
        fourth wall
       </a>
       and "appearing suddenly in unexpected places",
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-faust_dev_24-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-faust_dev-24">
         [23]
        </a>
       </sup>
       as well as an ability to
       <a href="/wiki/Precognition" title="Precognition">
        predict future events
       </a>
       through various body reactions, which she calls the "Pinkie Sense". In early episodes, Faust worked to depict Pinkie as a "free spirit" to address concerns of the character being seen as too "hyper" and "ditzy". As the creative team grew more comfortable with Pinkie's character and humor, she became "really over-the-top strange and bordering on crazy, with a wacky cartoonish magic all her own."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-faust_dev_24-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-faust_dev-24">
         [23]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Rarity">
        Rarity
        <span id="Opalescence">
        </span>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Rarity">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Tabitha_St._Germain" title="Tabitha St. Germain">
         Tabitha St. Germain
        </a>
        , singing voice by
        <a href="/wiki/Kazumi_Evans" title="Kazumi Evans">
         Kazumi Evans
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Rarity is a white unicorn with a violet, curled mane, based on the "G1" ponies Glory and Sparkler,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25">
        <a href="#cite_note-25">
         [24]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and named after the "G3" pony. She is a ladylike fashionista who speaks with a
       <a href="/wiki/Mid-Atlantic_accent" title="Mid-Atlantic accent">
        Mid-Atlantic accent
       </a>
       and runs a
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Haute_couture" title="Haute couture">
         haute couture
        </a>
       </i>
       salon in Ponyville called Carousel Boutique. Despite her vain and melodramatic tendencies, she has a generous spirit and strives to create dresses that capture their wearers' inner beauty.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">
        <a href="#cite_note-26">
         [25]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">
        <a href="#cite_note-27">
         [26]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She owns a pet
       <a href="/wiki/Persian_cat" title="Persian cat">
        Persian cat
       </a>
       named Opalescence, commonly nicknamed Opal. Faust's original idea for Rarity's Element of Harmony was "inspiration", but it was changed to "generosity" after the production team deemed the former "too much of a thinker, especially for kids." Faust was pleased with the change, saying it "really helped pull [Rarity] away from the stereotypical, unlikable debutante."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-Elements_8-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-Elements-8">
         [8]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She cites
       <a href="/wiki/Audrey_Hepburn" title="Audrey Hepburn">
        Audrey Hepburn
       </a>
       as her biggest influence for Rarity,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">
        <a href="#cite_note-28">
         [27]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and also says that Tabitha St. Germain's performance "added a humor to Rarity that was unexpected and wonderful."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-faustint_23-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-faustint-23">
         [22]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Applejack">
        Applejack
        <span id="Winona">
        </span>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Applejack">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Ashleigh_Ball" title="Ashleigh Ball">
         Ashleigh Ball
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Applejack is an orange, blonde-haired earth pony based on the "G1" character of the same name.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">
        <a href="#cite_note-29">
         [28]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She is characterized as a "farm gal" who sports a cowboy hat and lasso, and speaks with a Southern accent.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-AJ_30-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-AJ-30">
         [29]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She works as an
       <a href="/wiki/Apple" title="Apple">
        apple
       </a>
       farmer at the Sweet Apple Acres
       <a href="/wiki/Orchard" title="Orchard">
        orchard
       </a>
       in Ponyville, using her great physical strength to "buck" apples out of trees. She lives with her grandmother Granny Smith, older brother Big McIntosh, younger sister Apple Bloom, and pet
       <a href="/wiki/Collie" title="Collie">
        collie
       </a>
       Winona; according to Faust, Applejack's parents – first depicted in season seven's "The Perfect Pear" as Bright Mac (voiced by Bill Newton) and Pear Butter (voiced by
       <a href="/wiki/Felicia_Day" title="Felicia Day">
        Felicia Day
       </a>
       ) – are deceased.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-faustq&amp;a_31-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-faustq&amp;a-31">
         [30]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Applejack is honest, reliable, and the most "down-to-earth" of the Mane Six.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-AJ_30-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-AJ-30">
         [29]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She also has a stubborn streak, with several episodes focusing on her taking up some sort of "herculean task".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">
        <a href="#cite_note-32">
         [31]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Author Begin says that her apple-themed cutie mark "not only represents her name, but also is a symbol of the down-home simplicity found in a classic and common fruit."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">
        <a href="#cite_note-33">
         [32]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Fluttershy">
        Fluttershy
        <span id="Angel">
        </span>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Fluttershy">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Libman" title="Andrea Libman">
         Andrea Libman
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Fluttershy is a yellow pegasus with a long, pink mane, based on the "G1" earth pony Posey.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">
        <a href="#cite_note-34">
         [33]
        </a>
       </sup>
       True to her name, she is "defined by her shy sweetness; soft, whispery voice; and tender, nurturing nature," as described by author Begin.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">
        <a href="#cite_note-35">
         [34]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She possesses a unique affinity for animals that allows her to understand and communicate with them. She lives in a secluded meadow cottage in Ponyville, where she cares for multiple woodland creatures such as her "conniving and willful" pet
       <a href="/wiki/Rabbit" title="Rabbit">
        rabbit
       </a>
       Angel Bunny.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-FS_36-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-FS-36">
         [35]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">
        <a href="#cite_note-37">
         [36]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In many episodes, Fluttershy exhibits a more authoritative personality that emerges whenever a friend or animal is harmed in some way, in contrast to her normally fearful and submissive self.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">
        <a href="#cite_note-38">
         [37]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Her most prominent ability is known as "the Stare", which causes any creature that meets her gaze to become "powerless and moved to meekness" while it is in effect.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">
        <a href="#cite_note-39">
         [38]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Faust enjoyed writing for Fluttershy the most out of the show's characters due to her "relatable" struggles with fear, which Faust says brings potential "not just for great storytelling but [also for] great filmmaking."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-faust_dev_24-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-faust_dev-24">
         [23]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Spike">
        Spike
        <span id="Peewee">
        </span>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Spike">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Cathy_Weseluck" title="Cathy Weseluck">
         Cathy Weseluck
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Spike the Dragon
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-SD_40-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-SD-40">
         [39]
        </a>
       </sup>
       is a purple baby
       <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">
        dragon
       </a>
       with green spines, based on the "G1" and "G3" character of the same name. Hatched from an egg by a young Twilight Sparkle as part of her entrance exam for Celestia's academy, he fulfills the role of Twilight's "number one assistant", named so for his loyalty and skill at helping Twilight solve problems and learn lessons.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-SD_40-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-SD-40">
         [39]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE-SD_41-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE-SD-41">
         [40]
        </a>
       </sup>
       He is also described as having "an incurable crush on Rarity, an insatiable appetite for sparkly gems, and the uniquely comical ability to messenger letters via his fiery dragon breath."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-SD_40-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-SD-40">
         [39]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Author Begin calls Spike a
       <a href="/wiki/Foil_(literature)" title="Foil (literature)">
        foil
       </a>
       to the Mane Six in terms of personality, size, and shape, which "provides plenty of opportunity for exploring this difference in story lines."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE-SD_41-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE-SD-41">
         [40]
        </a>
       </sup>
       He adopts a newborn
       <a href="/wiki/Phoenix_(mythology)" title="Phoenix (mythology)">
        phoenix
       </a>
       named Peewee as a pet in the second-season episode "Dragon Quest", later returning Peewee to his family in season three's "Just for Sidekicks". Faust envisioned the character as "the sensitive little boy who has a lot of sisters and just seems to get along better with girls."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">
        <a href="#cite_note-42">
         [41]
        </a>
       </sup>
       On Spike's role as a dragon outsider living among ponies, Meghan McCarthy says, "He's trying to figure out who he is. What beyond being Twilight's assistant is his role in this world? I think he really reflects how everybody feels at some point in their life."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-SD_40-3">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-SD-40">
         [39]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Secondary_characters">
        Secondary characters
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Secondary characters">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Princess_Celestia">
        Princess Celestia
        <span id="Philomena">
        </span>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Princess Celestia">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Nicole_Oliver" title="Nicole Oliver">
         Nicole Oliver
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Princess Celestia, based on the "G1" unicorn Majesty,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">
        <a href="#cite_note-43">
         [42]
        </a>
       </sup>
       is a regal white alicorn depicted as the benevolent ruler of Equestria. Her design is larger, more mature, and more horse-like than the standard pony character, and she has a flowing, multicolored mane and tail resembling a celestial body.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">
        <a href="#cite_note-44">
         [43]
        </a>
       </sup>
       As detailed in
       <i>
        The Journal of the Two Sisters
       </i>
       , Celestia has ruled Equestria for over one thousand years due to her kind's slowed aging, and her status as an alicorn is seen as a symbol of harmony between unicorns, pegasi and earth ponies.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jots_45-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-jots-45">
         [44]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She is responsible for magically raising the sun each day in the show's setting from her castle in Canterlot. She also acts as a mentor and, as described by Faust, "a bit of a surrogate parent" to Twilight Sparkle,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ms_faust_2-3">
        <a href="#cite_note-ms_faust-2">
         [2]
        </a>
       </sup>
       guiding her throughout the series' first three seasons to her eventual destiny as a princess of Equestria. She owns a mischievous pet
       <a href="/wiki/Phoenix_(mythology)" title="Phoenix (mythology)">
        phoenix
       </a>
       named Philomena, who appears to be a "squaking old bird" before bursting into flames and renewing herself.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">
        <a href="#cite_note-46">
         [45]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Faust's original concept for Celestia was a queen rather than a princess, reflecting her status as the "highest authority" in the series' setting. The change was made at Hasbro's statement that "girls assume that Queens are evil [...] and Princesses are good," and that "the perceived youth of a Princess is preferable to consumers."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47">
        <a href="#cite_note-47">
         [46]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Princess_Luna">
        Princess Luna
        <span id="Nightmare_Moon">
        </span>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Princess Luna">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Tabitha_St._Germain" title="Tabitha St. Germain">
         Tabitha St. Germain
        </a>
        , singing voice by
        <a href="/wiki/Kazumi_Evans" title="Kazumi Evans">
         Kazumi Evans
        </a>
        ("
        <a href="/wiki/Twilight%27s_Kingdom" title="Twilight's Kingdom">
         Twilight's Kingdom
        </a>
        ") and Aloma Steele ("
        <a href="/wiki/A_Hearth%27s_Warming_Tail" title="A Hearth's Warming Tail">
         A Hearth's Warming Tail
        </a>
        ")
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Princess Luna, also named "Selena" in earlier drafts, is a dark-blue alicorn and Princess Celestia's younger sister, designed and developed by
       <a href="/wiki/Lynne_Naylor" title="Lynne Naylor">
        Lynne Naylor
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-PL_48-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-PL-48">
         [47]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She serves as co-ruler of Equestria alongside Celestia, using her magic to maintain the
       <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">
        moon
       </a>
       and safeguard her subjects' dreams during nighttime. Luna is introduced as the opening episodes' antagonist Nightmare Moon, transformed into a malevolent, black-coated mare by bitterness and jealousy towards her more beloved sister; as expounded in the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_(comic_book)" title="My Little Pony: Friendship Is Magic (comic book)">
        comic series
       </a>
       , her alter ego is a creation of the Nightmare Forces, a dark lunar miasma that preys on Luna's insecurities to convince her to become their host.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">
        <a href="#cite_note-49">
         [48]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Banished to the moon by the reluctant Celestia in the series' past, Nightmare Moon returns from a millennial exile to evoke eternal night-time. The Mane Six use the Elements of Harmony to purify and reform Luna, who reconciles with her sister and resumes her royal duties in a weakened state. She sports a different design in later episodes with a darker coloration and starry mane, which represent her dominion over the night.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50">
        <a href="#cite_note-50">
         [49]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Several episodes depict Luna's "difficulty living in her older sister's shadow", such as adapting to modern Equestrian customs and repairing her public image.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-PL_48-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-PL-48">
         [47]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Outside the television series, Luna owns a pet
       <a href="/wiki/Opossum" title="Opossum">
        opossum
       </a>
       named Tiberius that appears in several comics and chapter books.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Cutie_Mark_Crusaders">
        Cutie Mark Crusaders
        <span id="Apple_Bloom">
        </span>
        <span id="Scootaloo">
        </span>
        <span id="Sweetie_Belle">
        </span>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Cutie Mark Crusaders">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The Cutie Mark Crusaders are a trio of fillies who are bonded by their desire to earn their "cutie marks", symbols that adorn a pony's flank once they discover their special talents in life.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AVClub_51-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AVClub-51">
         [50]
        </a>
       </sup>
       They are each depicted as younger sibling figures to the main cast except Scootaloo.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE87_52-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE87-52">
         [51]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Several episodes of the series focus on the Crusaders' misadventures in trying to earn their marks in "the most unorthodox and sometimes less-than-productive ways."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE87_52-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE87-52">
         [51]
        </a>
       </sup>
       This goal is achieved in the season five episode "Crusaders of the Lost Mark", where the members gain similarly-themed cutie marks when they recognize their true purpose in life is helping other ponies discover or interpret their own cutie marks. The Crusaders featured in the series are:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <b>
         Apple Bloom
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Michelle_Creber" title="Michelle Creber">
         Michelle Creber
        </a>
        ) – Apple Bloom is a yellow earth pony filly with red mane and a pink mane bow, and is named for being "full of potential" and having "a lot of growing to do." A fiesty girl with a sarcastic streak, she is the younger sister of Applejack and Big McIntosh who formulates and spearheads most of the Cutie Mark Crusaders' "missions".
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-CMC_53-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH-CMC-53">
          [52]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Scootaloo
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Madeleine_Peters" title="Madeleine Peters">
         Madeleine Peters
        </a>
        ) – Scootaloo is an orange pegasus filly with purple mane, based on the "G3" pony of the same name. She suffers from an inability to fly, and instead uses her wings to propel her specially fashioned scooter. She idolizes Rainbow Dash as an older sister figure, often trying to imitate Rainbow Dash's "too cool" attitude and athletic skill.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-CMC_53-1">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH-CMC-53">
          [52]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Sweetie Belle
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Claire_Corlett" title="Claire Corlett">
         Claire Corlett
        </a>
        , singing voice for seasons 1–3 by Michelle Creber)
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54">
         <a href="#cite_note-54">
          [53]
         </a>
        </sup>
        – Sweetie Belle is a "sweet-natured and sometimes spacey" unicorn filly with a white coat and a lavender and pink-striped mane, based on the "G3" pony of the same name. She has "a blossoming talent for singing", and strives to become a fashion designer and gain the approval of her older sister, Rarity.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-CMC_53-2">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH-CMC-53">
          [52]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Babs Seed
        </b>
        (voiced by Brynna Drummond) – Babs is an earth pony filly and "tough-talkin' Apple cousin from Manehattan", debuting in the third-season episode "One Bad Apple". The character was created as a "blank flank" bully of the Cutie Mark Crusaders "whose behavior was the result of an insecurity that the Crusaders could relate to and ultimately help her overcome". She joins the Crusaders and forms her own branch of the club in Manehattan because, according to McCarthy, "We've got our three Crusaders in Ponyville and didn't want to add a permanent fourth."
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-CMC_53-3">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH-CMC-53">
          [52]
         </a>
        </sup>
        Babs earns her cutie mark as a hairstylist in the season five episode "Bloom &amp; Gloom".
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Gabby
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Erin_Mathews" title="Erin Mathews">
         Erin Mathews
        </a>
        ) – Gabby is a friendly and enthusiastic female
        <a href="/wiki/Griffin" title="Griffin">
         griffon
        </a>
        featured in the show's sixth season. Introduced as a social outcast from the griffon city of Griffonstone, she joins the Crusaders at the end of her debut episode, "The Fault in Our Cutie Marks", following her failed attempts to obtain her own cutie mark.
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Discord">
        Discord
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Discord">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:John_de_lancie_bronycon_summer_2012_cropped.png">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1431" data-file-width="870" height="362" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/John_de_lancie_bronycon_summer_2012_cropped.png/220px-John_de_lancie_bronycon_summer_2012_cropped.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/John_de_lancie_bronycon_summer_2012_cropped.png/330px-John_de_lancie_bronycon_summer_2012_cropped.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/John_de_lancie_bronycon_summer_2012_cropped.png/440px-John_de_lancie_bronycon_summer_2012_cropped.png 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:John_de_lancie_bronycon_summer_2012_cropped.png" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Actor
         <a href="/wiki/John_de_Lancie" title="John de Lancie">
          John de Lancie
         </a>
         (pictured at
         <a href="/wiki/BronyCon" title="BronyCon">
          BronyCon
         </a>
         , 2012) voices Discord, a character based on his television role as
         <a href="/wiki/Q_(Star_Trek)" title="Q (Star Trek)">
          Q
         </a>
         from
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           Star Trek: The Next Generation
          </a>
         </i>
         .
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/John_de_Lancie" title="John de Lancie">
         John de Lancie
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Discord is a spirit of chaos who first appeared as the antagonist of the season two premiere "
       <a href="/wiki/The_Return_of_Harmony" title="The Return of Harmony">
        The Return of Harmony
       </a>
       ". Primarily characterized as a nonsensical
       <a href="/wiki/Trickster" title="Trickster">
        trickster
       </a>
       ,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55">
        <a href="#cite_note-55">
         [54]
        </a>
       </sup>
       he is a
       <a href="/wiki/Greek_mythology" title="Greek mythology">
        Greek mythology
       </a>
       -inspired
       <a href="/wiki/Mythological_hybrid" title="Mythological hybrid">
        creature
       </a>
       called a "draconequus"
       <span class="nowrap">
        <span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt">
         <a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">
          /
          <span style="border-bottom:1px dotted">
           <span title="'d' in 'dye'">
            d
           </span>
           <span title="'r' in 'rye'">
            r
           </span>
           <span title="/ə/: 'a' in 'about'">
            ə
           </span>
           <span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">
            ˈ
           </span>
           <span title="'k' in 'kind'">
            k
           </span>
           <span title="/ɒ/: 'o' in 'body'">
            ɒ
           </span>
           <span title="'n' in 'nigh'">
            n
           </span>
           <span title="/ɛ/: 'e' in 'dress'">
            ɛ
           </span>
           <span title="'k' in 'kind'">
            k
           </span>
           <span title="'w' in 'wind'">
            w
           </span>
           <span title="/ʌ/: 'u' in 'cut'">
            ʌ
           </span>
           <span title="'s' in 'sigh'">
            s
           </span>
          </span>
          /
         </a>
        </span>
       </span>
       (from the Latin words meaning "dragon horse"), a serpentine being with a pony's head and numerous different animal parts, which is meant to symbolize his inharmonious nature.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH54_56-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH54-56">
         [55]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE3132_57-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE3132-57">
         [56]
        </a>
       </sup>
       He is shown to be opposed by Princesses Celestia and Luna in the series' distant past for tormenting ponies with his reality-bending powers, and he similarly faces the Mane Six during the premiere; both times, the ponies use the Elements of Harmony to turn him into stone. In the season three episode "Keep Calm and Flutter On", Discord is released under Celestia's decree to reform himself, which he does after Fluttershy treats him like a friend. He appears in later episodes as a reluctant ally of the Mane Six, occasionally causing mischief while struggling to become a better friend to them.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH54_56-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH54-56">
         [55]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Faust based Discord's character on
       <a href="/wiki/Q_(Star_Trek)" title="Q (Star Trek)">
        Q
       </a>
       , an omnipotent trickster played by John de Lancie on the television series
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
         Star Trek: The Next Generation
        </a>
       </i>
       . The production team considered casting a soundalike of de Lancie to voice the character, and were surprised to learn that de Lancie himself was available.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DisQord_58-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-DisQord-58">
         [57]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The creative team developed Discord as "the one character who could break all of the rules of the show" by including more modern or contemporary references than usual in the series' "fantasy storybook" setting.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE-DC_59-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE-DC-59">
         [58]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60">
        <a href="#cite_note-60">
         [59]
        </a>
       </sup>
       He was not intended to have a recurring role;
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoE-DC_59-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoE-DC-59">
         [58]
        </a>
       </sup>
       according to McCarthy, "'reforming' him allows us to tell new stories with his character. He gets to be the not-always-reliable ally instead of the known enemy."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH54_56-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH54-56">
         [55]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Author Begin commented on the "chaotic" settings that accompany the character, such as his home dimension called Chaosville, likening them to "dream-inspired
       <a href="/wiki/Salvador_Dal%C3%AD" title="Salvador Dalí">
        Salvador Dalí
       </a>
       paintings."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61">
        <a href="#cite_note-61">
         [60]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Princess_Cadance_and_Shining_Armor">
        <span id="Princess_Cadance">
         Princess Cadance
        </span>
        and
        <span id="Shining_Armor">
         Shining Armor
        </span>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Princess Cadance and Shining Armor">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Britt_McKillip" title="Britt McKillip">
         Britt McKillip
        </a>
        (Princess Cadance) and
        <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Francis" title="Andrew Francis">
         Andrew Francis
        </a>
        (Shining Armor)
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Princess Cadance and Shining Armor are Twilight Sparkle's older sister-in-law and brother, respectively, who both debuted in the season two finale "
       <a href="/wiki/A_Canterlot_Wedding" title="A Canterlot Wedding">
        A Canterlot Wedding
       </a>
       ". Cadance, a kindhearted alicorn who is fully named Princess Mi Amore Cadenza, is Princess Celestia's adopted niece and Twilight's childhood "foal-sitter" (
       <a href="/wiki/Babysitting" title="Babysitting">
        babysitter
       </a>
       );
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-CS_62-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-CS-62">
         [61]
        </a>
       </sup>
       according to her backstory presented in
       <i>
        Twilight Sparkle and the Crystal Heart Spell
       </i>
       , Cadance is a former pegasus who turned into an alicorn after reversing an evil sorceress's love-stealing spell.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63">
        <a href="#cite_note-63">
         [62]
        </a>
       </sup>
       She marries the unicorn Shining Armor, who is the captain of Canterlot's royal guard and has a close relationship with his sister, for which he is nicknamed her "Big Brother Best Friend Forever" (B.B.B.F.F.).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH-CS_62-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH-CS-62">
         [61]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In the
       <a href="/wiki/The_Crystal_Empire" title="The Crystal Empire">
        third-season premiere
       </a>
       , Celestia appoints Shining Armor and Cadance to rule the Crystal Empire, an "ancient city" that Cadance protects using the power of love so that their subjects, the shimmering coated "crystal ponies", may magically project their feelings of hope and love across Equestria.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH71_64-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-EoH71-64">
         [63]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In the season six premiere "The Crystalling", Cadance gives birth to an alicorn filly named Flurry Heart (voiced by
       <a href="/wiki/Tabitha_St._Germain" title="Tabitha St. Germain">
        Tabitha St. Germain
       </a>
       ).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65">
        <a href="#cite_note-65">
         [64]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Starlight_Glimmer">
        Starlight Glimmer
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Starlight Glimmer">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Kelly_Sheridan" title="Kelly Sheridan">
         Kelly Sheridan
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Starlight Glimmer is a unicorn who debuted in the season five premiere "
       <a href="/wiki/The_Cutie_Map" title="The Cutie Map">
        The Cutie Map
       </a>
       ". Initially appearing as a "perfectly pleasant-looking unicorn", Starlight proves to be a sinister figure who wishes to build a "perfectly equal society" by using her magic to remove other ponies' cutie marks; she cites her reasons as believing that differing degrees of ability cause disharmony between friends,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoH108_66-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoH108-66">
         [65]
        </a>
       </sup>
       stemming from her estrangement from her childhood friend Sunburst (voiced by Ian Hanlin) after he earns his cutie mark before her. She later appears in the season finale "The Cutie Re-Mark" to take revenge against the Mane Six by
       <a href="/wiki/Time_travel" title="Time travel">
        traveling to the past
       </a>
       and preventing their friendship before it starts. After realizing the catastrophic changes this causes in the present, Starlight is convinced to change her ways and make new friends. She appears in season six as Twilight's pupil who studies friendship alongside the Mane Six in Ponyville, a role she graduates from in the season seven episode "Celestial Advice". According to Miller, Starlight's design was chosen to parallel her role as a "proto-Twilight character".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoH108_66-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoH108-66">
         [65]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Her original name during production was "Aurora Glimmer", which was changed due to the
       <a href="/wiki/The_Walt_Disney_Company" title="The Walt Disney Company">
        Walt Disney Company
       </a>
       's trademark of the character name "
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aurora_(Disney_character)" title="Aurora (Disney character)">
        Aurora
       </a>
       ".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67">
        <a href="#cite_note-67">
         [66]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Recurring_characters">
        Recurring characters
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Recurring characters">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Ponyville_characters">
        Ponyville characters
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Ponyville characters">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Ponyville is the primary setting of the television series and home of the show's main characters. The town's unique locales were designed to reflect their characters, while the overall style of the town was largely influenced by
       <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania_Dutch" title="Pennsylvania Dutch">
        Pennsylvania Dutch
       </a>
       design,
       <a href="/wiki/Steampunk" title="Steampunk">
        steampunk
       </a>
       artwork, and
       <a href="/wiki/European_folklore" title="European folklore">
        European
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Bavaria" title="Bavaria">
        Bavarian folklore
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoH140_68-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoH140-68">
         [67]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The town also incorporates pony design elements such as horseshoes, hay bales, and troughs.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoH142143_69-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoH142143-69">
         [68]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Big_Macintosh">
         </span>
         <span id="Big_Mac">
         </span>
         <span id="Big_McIntosh">
          Big McIntosh
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Peter_New" title="Peter New">
         Peter New
        </a>
        ) – Big McIntosh, commonly called Big Mac, is a large earth pony stallion who is Applejack and Apple Bloom's older brother. He "generally doesn't have much to say", and often speaks only by replying "eeyup" and "nope".
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH28_70-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH28-70">
          [69]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Granny_Smith">
          Granny Smith
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Tabitha_St._Germain" title="Tabitha St. Germain">
         Tabitha St. Germain
        </a>
        ) – Granny Smith is the earth pony grandmother of Applejack, Apple Bloom, and Big McIntosh. She is depicted as a "wise matriarch" who has sharp wit and a "fuzzy" memory, and she is stated to be one of Ponyville's first settlers.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH28_70-1">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH28-70">
          [69]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Mayor_Mare">
          Mayor Mare
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Cathy_Weseluck" title="Cathy Weseluck">
         Cathy Weseluck
        </a>
        ) – Mayor Mare is the earth pony mayor of Ponyville.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH29_71-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH29-71">
          [70]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Mr._Cake">
         </span>
         <span id="Mrs._Cake">
         </span>
         <span id="Pound_Cake">
         </span>
         <span id="Pumpkin_Cake">
         </span>
         <span id="Cake_family">
          Cake family
         </span>
        </b>
        – Mr. Carrot Cake (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Brian_Drummond" title="Brian Drummond">
         Brian Drummond
        </a>
        ) and Mrs. Cup Cake (voiced by Tabitha St. Germain), both earth ponies, are the owners of the Sugarcube Corner bakery. In the season two episode "Baby Cakes", Mrs. Cake gives birth to twin foals, a pegasus colt named Pound (voiced by St. Germain), and a unicorn filly named Pumpkin (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Libman" title="Andrea Libman">
         Andrea Libman
        </a>
        ).
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH29_71-1">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH29-71">
          [70]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Cheerilee">
          Cheerilee
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Nicole_Oliver" title="Nicole Oliver">
         Nicole Oliver
        </a>
        ) – Cheerilee is an earth pony based on the "G3" toy of the same name, appearing as a schoolteacher at the Ponyville Schoolhouse.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH29_71-2">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH29-71">
          [70]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Snips">
         </span>
         <span id="Snails">
         </span>
         <span id="Snips_and_Snails">
          Snips and Snails
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Lee_Tockar" title="Lee Tockar">
         Lee Tockar
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Richard_Ian_Cox" title="Richard Ian Cox">
         Richard Ian Cox
        </a>
        ) – Snips and Snails are a pair of dimwitted unicorn colts who create mischief in Ponyville. The short and pudgy Snips is "known for his enthusiasm", while the taller Snails is "slightly more relaxed".
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH40_72-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH40-72">
          [71]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Diamond_Tiara">
         </span>
         <span id="Silver_Spoon">
         </span>
         <span id="Filthy_Rich">
         </span>
         <span id="Spoiled_Rich">
         </span>
         <span id="Diamond_Tiara_and_Silver_Spoon">
          Diamond Tiara and Silver Spoon
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Chantal_Strand" title="Chantal Strand">
         Chantal Strand
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Shannon_Chan-Kent" title="Shannon Chan-Kent">
         Shannon Chan-Kent
        </a>
        ) – Diamond Tiara and her cohort Silver Spoon are two wealthy, snobbish earth pony fillies who tease the Cutie Mark Crusaders for not having their cutie marks, calling them "blank flanks".
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH40_72-1">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH40-72">
          [71]
         </a>
        </sup>
        It is shown in "Crusaders of the Lost Mark" that Diamond Tiara's behavior stems from her stress about meeting the expectations of her father Filthy Rich (voiced by Brian Drummond) and mother Spoiled Rich (voiced by Strand), who are practically the reason for her snobbiness. By the episode's end, she and Silver Spoon make peace with the Crusaders.
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Pip_Squeak">
         </span>
         <span id="Pip">
         </span>
         <span id="Pipsqueak">
          Pipsqueak
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by William Lawrenson in "Luna Eclipsed" and
        <a href="/wiki/Graham_Verchere" title="Graham Verchere">
         Graham Verchere
        </a>
        in all other appearances) – Pipsqueak, also named Pip, is a
        <a href="/wiki/Pinto_horse" title="Pinto horse">
         pinto
        </a>
        earth pony colt who hails from Trottingham, a location outside of Ponyville.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH40_72-2">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH40-72">
          [71]
         </a>
        </sup>
        He speaks with a Cockney accent in most of his appearances.
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Cranky_Doodle_Donkey">
         </span>
         <span id="Cranky_Doodle">
         </span>
         <span id="Matilda">
         </span>
         <span id="Cranky_Doodle_and_Matilda">
          Cranky Doodle and Matilda
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Richard_Newman_(actor)" title="Richard Newman (actor)">
         Richard Newman
        </a>
        and Brenda Crichlow) – Cranky Doodle Donkey is a
        <a href="/wiki/Donkey" title="Donkey">
         donkey
        </a>
        and "crotchety old grouch" who rejects Pinkie Pie's friendship until she reunites him with his long-lost "special friend" Matilda, a female donkey.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH4445_73-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH4445-73">
          [72]
         </a>
        </sup>
        The two marry in the one-hundredth episode "
        <a href="/wiki/Slice_of_Life_(My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic)" title="Slice of Life (My Little Pony: Friendship Is Magic)">
         Slice of Life
        </a>
        ".
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Bulk_Biceps">
          Bulk Biceps
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by Jayson Thiessen/
        <a href="/wiki/Michael_Dobson_(actor)" title="Michael Dobson (actor)">
         Michael Dobson
        </a>
        ) – Bulk Biceps is a muscular pegasus stallion with small wings. His design was partially based on
        <a href="/wiki/John_Kricfalusi" title="John Kricfalusi">
         John Kricfalusi
        </a>
        's animation style.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74">
         <a href="#cite_note-74">
          [73]
         </a>
        </sup>
        He first appears as a nameless gag character in the season two episode "Hurricane Fluttershy", where his shouts of "Yeah!" (attributed to "pony
        <a href="/wiki/Walla" title="Walla">
         walla
        </a>
        ") are recorded by Thiessen.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75">
         <a href="#cite_note-75">
          [74]
         </a>
        </sup>
        Dobson performs the character in full speaking appearances starting with season four's "Rainbow Falls".
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Canterlot_characters">
        Canterlot characters
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Canterlot characters">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Canterlot is the mountainside capital of Equestria, named after the castle
       <a href="/wiki/Camelot" title="Camelot">
        Camelot
       </a>
       of
       <a href="/wiki/King_Arthur" title="King Arthur">
        Arthurian legend
       </a>
       . The city is home to the country's upper-class elite, including Princess Celestia and Princess Luna, who reside in the local castle. Canterlot was designed to give the sense of its residents' royalty and nobility.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AoH162_76-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-AoH162-76">
         [75]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Prince_Blueblood">
          Prince Blueblood
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Tong" title="Vincent Tong">
         Vincent Tong
        </a>
        ) – Blueblood is Princess Celestia's unicorn nephew and an object of Rarity's affections in the first season until he proves to be "quite vain" and "a pompous fool".
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH33_77-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH33-77">
          [76]
         </a>
        </sup>
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">
         <a href="#cite_note-78">
          [77]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Hoity_Toity">
          Hoity Toity
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Trevor_Devall" title="Trevor Devall">
         Trevor Devall
        </a>
        ) – Hoity Toity is an earth pony "fashion guru" who gives make-or-break critiques to designers.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH32_79-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH32-79">
          [78]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Photo_Finish">
          Photo Finish
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Tabitha_St._Germain" title="Tabitha St. Germain">
         Tabitha St. Germain
        </a>
        ) – Photo Finish is a famed earth pony fashion photographer who speaks with an Austrian accent.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH32_79-1">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH32-79">
          [78]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Sapphire_Shores">
          Sapphire Shores
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by Rena Anakwe) – Sapphire is an earth pony singer known as the "Pony of Pop", based on the "G3" toy of the same name.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH32_79-2">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH32-79">
          [78]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Fancypants">
         </span>
         <span id="Fancy_Pants">
          Fancy Pants
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by Trevor Devall) – Fancy Pants is a good-natured unicorn
        <a href="/wiki/Socialite" title="Socialite">
         socialite
        </a>
        with the highest position in elite Canterlot society, often appearing with a readily agreeable entourage.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoH32_79-3">
         <a href="#cite_note-EoH32-79">
          [78]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Sassy_Saddles">
          Sassy Saddles
         </span>
        </b>
        (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Kelly_Sheridan" title="Kelly Sheridan">
         Kelly Sheridan
        </a>
        ) – Sassy is the unicorn manager of Canterlot Carousel, Rarity's boutique in Canterlot that opens in the season five episode "Canterlot Boutique". Her design was inspired by
        <a href="/wiki/Emily_Blunt" title="Emily Blunt">
         Emily Blunt
        </a>
        's character Emily Charlton in
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/The_Devil_Wears_Prada_(film)" title="The Devil Wears Prada (film)">
          The Devil Wears Prada
         </a>
        </i>
        .
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80">
         <a href="#cite_note-80">
          [79]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Cloudsdale_characters">
        Cloudsdale characters
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_My_Little_Pony:_Friendship_Is_Magic_characters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Cloudsdale characters">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Cloudsdale is the home and birthplace of several pegasus characters such as Rainbow Dash and Fluttershy. It is depicted as a floating city of clouds where pegasi produce Equestria's clouds, weather and
       <a href="/wiki/Rainbow" title="Rainbow">
        rainbows
       </a>
       inside a specialized "weather factory".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81">
        <a href="#cite_note-81">
         [80]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The city's design was influenced by
       <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Greek_architecture" title="Ancient Greek architecture">
        Greek
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Roman_architecture" title="Ancient Roman architecture">
        Roman architecture
       </a>
       , which author Begin states "harks back to the original Olympic Games, [...] a fitting reference for Rainbow Dash."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82">
        <a href="#cite_note-82">
         [81]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <b>
         <span id="Spitfire">
         </span>
         <span id="Soarin">
         </span>
         <span id="Blaze">
         </span>
         <span id="Fleetfoot">
         </span>
         <span id="Misty_Fly">
         </span>
         <span id="The_Wonderbolts">
          The Wonderbolts
         </span>
        </b>
        – The Wonderbolts are a squad of pegasi that perform "aerial feats of wonder", based on the
        <a href="/wiki/Blue_Angels" title="Blue Angels">
         Blue Angels
        </a>
        .
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83">
         <a href="#cite_note-83">
          [82]
         </a>
        </sup>
        They are captained by Spitfire (voiced by
        <a href="/wiki/Nicole_Oliver" title="Nicole Oliver">
         Nicole Oliver
        </a>
        in the episode "Sonic Rainboom" and
